<h3 class="sr-hotel__title " data-et-click="customGoal:OQRWSEcYC:4">
<a class="hotel_name_link url" data-et-click="
" href="/hotel/jp/nazuna-kyoto-higashiyama-tei-warmth-functional.zh-tw.html?label=gen173nr-1DCAEoggJCAlhYSDNiBW5vcmVmaOcBiAEBmAEwuAEGyAEM2AED6AEBkgIBeagCAw;sid=4996667e149bfae490c17f2eb37eafa9;checkin=2017-09-07;checkout=2017-09-11;ucfs=1;srpvid=c169246cfc260203;highlighted_blocks=221467701_103672419_2_0_0;all_sr_blocks=221467701_103672419_2_0_0;room1=A%2CA;hpos=5;dest_type=city;dest_id=-235402;srfid=896ff784ef3dbb6a8db0bb8d04e6e6b8350cc3b4X105;from=searchresults;highlight_room=#hotelTmpl" rel="noopener" target="_blank">

度假屋
</span>

<span class="invisible_spoken">2 星級</span></i>
<i class="preferred-program-icon bicon-thumb-up jq_tooltip pp-icon-medium-sr" data-hash="aDMDcTBeNDUfcXIFdXC" data-stage="1" rel="300" style="font-size: 20px" title="此住宿已同意參與我們的首選住宿計畫。首選住宿以優惠價格為顧客提供最卓越且具高性價比的服務。參與此計畫的住宿業者必須符合特定標準，曾入住顧客之意見亦會納入評估考量。">
<span class="invisible_spoken">此住宿已同意參與我們的首選住宿計畫。首選住宿以優惠價格為顧客提供最卓越且具高性價比的服務。參與此計畫的住宿業者必須符合特定標準，曾入住顧客之意見亦會納入評估考量。</span></i>
